## Overall Closure Bar

- overall verdict: `still_open`
- closure bar: the rollout stays open until every source row currently marked `Open`, `Partial`, or `Contract-undefined` has row-specific implementation, tests, or exact evidence, and the source matrix records `Closed` or `Covered` for that same row id with concrete files, commands, and gate outcomes.
- implementation-committed rule: unresolved row-owned sessions must not finish as acceptance-only, evidence-only, or doc-only cleanup when code or tests are needed.
- residual rule: `accepted_with_explicit_follow_up` is not an acceptable final row outcome for any source row that remains `Open`, `Partial`, or `Contract-undefined`.
- broad-rollout rule: broader residual truth-alignment, older accepted residuals, or subsystem-level closure notes are not substitutes for row-owned code/test/evidence closure.
- covered row rule: a row may stay `covered_in_repo` only while the exact current code and tests named for that row still close that exact row; contradictory evidence reopens the row-owned session.
- unsupported rows rule: rows classified `unsupported_product_scope` are out of current implementation scope and must remain non-gating unless the product contract changes.
- evidence rows rule: rows classified `repo_external_proof` or `needs_repo_evidence` must not be marked closed by adjacent host tests alone; they need the named Go, raw-protocol, simulator, device-lab, relay, packet-capture, or privacy proof called out by the row.
- row-owned truth rule: later closure must report final truth per source row id, not only per subsystem, smoke suite, or broad feature area.

## Row Traceability Rule

- Every source row maps to exactly one session id in this artifact.
- No source row maps to `duplicate_of`; the matrix has no duplicate Test IDs.
- Session ids preserve the source row ids verbatim because every row id is filename-safe.
- Later closure work must report final truth per source row, not only per broad subsystem, smoke suite, or rollout residual.

## Downstream Execution Path

1. Run `$implementation-session-pipeline-orchestrator` on this artifact when executing the rollout.
2. For each row-owned session, create or refresh the doc-scoped plan path `libp2p_group_chat_missing_test_matrix_full_with_rules-session-<session-id>-plan.md`.
3. Execute sessions in the ordered breakdown unless a fresh dependency pass identifies a real blocker. Do not merge row sessions by subsystem after this decomposition.
4. For `implementation-ready` rows, land code/tests or tests-only closure according to the row disposition and run the direct gates listed in that row entry.
5. For `evidence-gated` rows, collect the named Go, raw-protocol, real-network, simulator, relay, packet-capture, or device-lab proof first; if current behavior fails, convert only that row into targeted code/test work.
6. For `covered_in_repo` rows, do not create implementation work unless a direct rerun or code inspection contradicts the current matrix-named evidence.
7. For `unsupported_product_scope` rows, keep them non-gating unless product scope changes; if scope changes, update the source row and regenerate this breakdown.
8. A row-owned session is not done until the source matrix row is updated from an unresolved state to `Closed` or `Covered` with concrete evidence.
9. Update `Test-Flight-Improv/Group-Chat-Feature/test-inventory.md`, the source matrix, and any gate docs only as part of the executing row session, not during decomposition.
10. Keep the overall artifact verdict `still_open` until there are no source rows left marked `Open`, `Partial`, or `Contract-undefined`.
